收到。最终版接口确认：

```csharp
public interface IExchange : IDisposable
{
    void Send(byte[] data);
    byte[]? ReadExactly(int count);   // 读满返回，断开返回 null
    void Close();                      // Dispose() 内部调 Close()，可重复调用
    bool IsConnected { get; }
}
```

For FrameCodec, I need to migrate from Server/FrameCodec.cs and add IExchange overloads.

Let me think about the FrameCodec with IExchange:

```csharp
public static class FrameCodec
{
    private static readonly byte[] Magic = { 0xEB, 0x90 };

    // byte[] versions (keep existing)
    public static void SendFrame(NetworkStream stream, byte[] payload) { ... }
    public static byte[]? ReceiveFrame(NetworkStream stream) { ... }
    
    // IExchange versions (new)
    public static void SendFrame(IExchange exchange, byte[] payload)
    {
        byte[] lenBytes = LengthToBytes(payload.LongLength);
        byte[] frame = new byte[2 + lenBytes.Length + payload.Length];
        Array.Copy(Magic, 0, frame, 0, 2);
        Array.Copy(lenBytes, 0, frame, 2, lenBytes.Length);
        Array.Copy(payload, 0, frame, 2 + lenBytes.Length, payload.Length);
        exchange.Send(frame);
    }
    
    public static byte[]? ReceiveFrame(IExchange exchange)
    {
        byte[] magic = exchange.ReadExactly(2);
        if (magic == null) return null;
        if (magic[0] != 0xEB || magic[1] != 0x90)
            throw new Exception($"...");
        
        // Read variable length
        var lenList = new List<byte>();
        while (true)
        {
            byte[] b = exchange.ReadExactly(1);
            if (b == null) return null;
            lenList.Add(b[0]);
            if ((b[0] & 0x80) == 0) break;
        }
        long length = BytesToLength(lenList.ToArray());
        
        if (length == 0) return Array.Empty<byte>();
        if (length > int.MaxValue) throw new Exception($"...");
        
        return exchange.ReadExactly((int)length);
    }
    
    // ... LengthToBytes, BytesToLength unchanged
}
```

For StreamExchange:
```csharp
public class StreamExchange : IExchange
{
    private readonly NetworkStream _stream;
    
    public StreamExchange(NetworkStream stream)
    {
        _stream = stream;
    }
    
    public bool IsConnected => ... ; // Poll the socket
    
    public void Send(byte[] data)
    {
        _stream.Write(data, 0, data.Length);
        _stream.Flush();
    }
    
    public byte[]? ReadExactly(int count)
    {
        byte[] buffer = new byte[count];
        int total = 0;
        while (total < count)
        {
            int n = _stream.Read(buffer, total, count - total);
            if (n == 0) return null;
            total += n;
        }
        return buffer;
    }
    
    public void Close()
    {
        try { _stream.Close(); } catch { }
    }
    
    public void Dispose()
    {
        Close();
    }
}
```

For Client/Net.cs:
```csharp
namespace NetLab.Client
{
    public static class Net
    {
        public delegate IExchange CreateExchangeFunc(string ip, int port);
        public static CreateExchangeFunc? CreateExchange = null;
        
        public static byte[]? Send(string ip, int port, IAsdu asdu)
        {
            if (CreateExchange == null)
                throw new InvalidOperationException("CreateExchange 未注册");
            
            using IExchange exchange = CreateExchange(ip, port);
            FrameCodec.SendFrame(exchange, asdu.GetContent());
            return FrameCodec.ReceiveFrame(exchange);
        }
    }
}
```

Wait, for the IExchange-based FrameCodec methods, they're in NetLab.Common, but they need to use IExchange which is in the same assembly. That's fine.

For the NetworkStream-based methods, they need System.Net.Sockets. But since NetLab.Common is a library, it can reference the appropriate packages.

```csharp
private void HandleClient(TcpClient client)
{
    try
    {
        using NetworkStream stream = client.GetStream();
        using IExchange exchange = new StreamExchange(stream);
        
        while (true)
        {
            byte[]? payload = FrameCodec.ReceiveFrame(exchange);
            if (payload == null) break;
            
            // ... log ...
            
            IAsdu asdu = new BinaryAsdu(payload);
            FrameCodec.SendFrame(exchange, asdu.GetContent());
            // ... log ...
        }
    }
    catch ...
}

```csharp
// Client/EchoClient.cs
public class EchoClient
{
    public void RunTest()
    {
        Net.CreateExchange = CreateExchange;
        
        // Method 1: Direct IExchange (multi-message on one connection)
        using IExchange exchange = Net.CreateExchange("127.0.0.1", 9000);
        for (int i = 0; i < 3; i++)
        {
            IAsdu msg = new BinaryAsdu(Encoding.UTF8.GetBytes(...));
            FrameCodec.SendFrame(exchange, msg.GetContent());
            byte[]? response = FrameCodec.ReceiveFrame(exchange);
            ...
        }
        
        // Method 2: Net.Send (one request per connection)
        IAsdu singleMsg = new BinaryAsdu(...);
        byte[]? result = Net.Send("127.0.0.1", 9000, singleMsg);
    }
    
    private static IExchange CreateExchange(string host, int port)
    {
        TcpClient client = new TcpClient(host, port);
        return new StreamExchange(client.GetStream());
    }
}
```

  "content": "using System.Net.Sockets;\n\nnamespace NetLab.Common.Exchange\n{\n    public class StreamExchange : IExchange\n    {\n        private readonly NetworkStream _stream;\n        private readonly Socket _socket;\n\n        public StreamExchange(NetworkStream stream)\n        {\n            _stream = stream;\n            _socket = stream.Socket;\n        }\n\n        public bool IsConnected\n        {\n            get\n            {\n                try\n                {\n                    return !(_socket.Poll(0, SelectMode.SelectRead) && _socket.Available == 0);\n                }\n                catch\n                {\n                    return false;\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        public void Send(byte[] data)\n        {\n            _stream.Write(data, 0, data.Length);\n            _stream.Flush();\n        }\n\n        public byte[]? ReadExactly(int count)\n        {\n            byte[] buffer = new byte[count];\n            int total = 0;\n            while (total < count)\n            {\n                int n = _stream.Read(buffer, total, count - total);\n                if (n == 0) return null;\n                total += n;\n            }\n            return buffer;\n        }\n\n        public void Close()\n        {\n            try { _stream.Close(); } catch { }\n        }\n\n        public void Dispose()\n        {\n            Close();\n        }\n    }\n}\n",

**Tool: write**

**Input:**
```json
{
  "content": "using System.Net.Sockets;\nusing NetLab.Common.Exchange;\n\nnamespace NetLab.Common\n{\n    public static class FrameCodec\n    {\n        private static readonly byte[] Magic = { 0xEB, 0x90 };\n\n        // ===== NetworkStream 版本（保留，兼容旧代码） =====\n\n        public static void SendFrame(NetworkStream stream, byte[] payload)\n        {\n            stream.Write(Magic, 0, 2);\n            byte[] lenBytes = LengthToBytes(payload.LongLength);\n            stream.Write(lenBytes, 0, lenBytes.Length);\n            stream.Write(payload, 0, payload.Length);\n            stream.Flush();\n        }\n\n        public static byte[]? ReceiveFrame(NetworkStream stream)\n        {\n            byte[] magic = new byte[2];\n            if (ReadExactly(stream, magic, 2) != 2)\n                return null;\n            if (magic[0] != 0xEB || magic[1] != 0x90)\n                throw new Exception($\"帧头错误: {magic[0]:X2} {magic[1]:X2}\");\n\n            return ReadPayload(stream);\n        }\n\n        private static byte[]? ReadPayload(NetworkStream stream)\n        {\n            var lenList = new List<byte>();\n            while (true)\n            {\n                byte[] b = new byte[1];\n                if (ReadExactly(stream, b, 1) != 1)\n                    return null;\n                lenList.Add(b[0]);\n                if ((b[0] & 0x80) == 0) break;\n            }\n            long length = BytesToLength(lenList.ToArray());\n\n            if (length == 0) return Array.Empty<byte>();\n            if (length > int.MaxValue)\n                throw new Exception($\"载荷过大: {length}\");\n            byte[] payload = new byte[length];\n            if (ReadExactly(stream, payload, (int)length) != length)\n                return null;\n            return payload;\n        }\n\n        private static int ReadExactly(NetworkStream stream, byte[] buffer, int count)\n        {\n            int total = 0;\n            while (total < count)\n            {\n                int n = stream.Read(buffer, total, count - total);\n                if (n == 0) return total;\n                total += n;\n            }\n            return total;\n        }\n\n        // ===== IExchange 版本（新增 — Phase 2 核心） =====\n\n        public static void SendFrame(IExchange exchange, byte[] payload)\n        {\n            byte[] lenBytes = LengthToBytes(payload.LongLength);\n            byte[] frame = new byte[2 + lenBytes.Length + payload.Length];\n            Array.Copy(Magic, 0, frame, 0, 2);\n            Array.Copy(lenBytes, 0, frame, 2, lenBytes.Length);\n            Array.Copy(payload, 0, frame, 2 + lenBytes.Length, payload.Length);\n            exchange.Send(frame);\n        }\n\n        public static byte[]? ReceiveFrame(IExchange exchange)\n        {\n            byte[]? magic = exchange.ReadExactly(2);\n            if (magic == null) return null;\n            if (magic[0] != 0xEB || magic[1] != 0x90)\n                throw new Exception($\"帧头错误: {magic[0]:X2} {magic[1]:X2}\");\n\n            return ReadPayload(exchange);\n        }\n\n        private static byte[]? ReadPayload(IExchange exchange)\n        {\n            var lenList = new List<byte>();\n            while (true)\n            {\n                byte[]? b = exchange.ReadExactly(1);\n                if (b == null) return null;\n                lenList.Add(b[0]);\n                if ((b[0] & 0x80) == 0) break;\n            }\n            long length = BytesToLength(lenList.ToArray());\n\n            if (length == 0) return Array.Empty<byte>();\n            if (length > int.MaxValue)\n                throw new Exception($\"载荷过大: {length}\");\n            return exchange.ReadExactly((int)length);\n        }\n\n        // ===== 变长编码（公共） =====\n\n        public static byte[] LengthToBytes(long length)\n        {\n            if (length == 0) return new byte[] { 0x00 };\n\n            var bytes = new List<byte>();\n            while (length > 0)\n            {\n                bytes.Add((byte)(length & 0x7F));\n                length >>= 7;\n            }\n            bytes.Reverse();\n            for (int i = 0; i < bytes.Count - 1; i++)\n                bytes[i] |= 0x80;\n            return bytes.ToArray();\n        }\n\n        public static long BytesToLength(byte[] bytes)\n        {\n            long n = 0;\n            for (int i = 0; i < bytes.Length; i++)\n            {\n                n <<= 7;\n                n |= (long)(bytes[i] & 0x7F);\n            }\n            return n;\n        }\n    }\n}\n",
  "filePath": "D:\\code\\lab\\NetLab\\NetLab.Common\\FrameCodec.cs"
}
```

**Output:**
```
<path>D:\code\lab\NetLab\Protocol\FrameCodec.cs</path>
<type>file</type>
<content>
1: using System.Net.Sockets;
2: 
3: namespace NetLab.Protocol
4: {
5:     public static class FrameCodec
6:     {
7:         private static readonly byte[] Magic = { 0xEB, 0x90 };
8: 
9:         public static void SendFrame(NetworkStream stream, byte[] payload)
10:         {
11:             stream.Write(Magic, 0, 2);
12:             byte[] lenBytes = LengthToBytes(payload.LongLength);
13:             stream.Write(lenBytes, 0, lenBytes.Length);
14:             stream.Write(payload, 0, payload.Length);
15:             stream.Flush();
16:         }
17: 
18:         public static byte[]? ReceiveFrame(NetworkStream stream)
19:         {
20:             byte[] magic = new byte[2];
21:             if (ReadExactly(stream, magic, 2) != 2)
22:                 return null;
23:             if (magic[0] != 0xEB || magic[1] != 0x90)
24:                 throw new Exception($"帧头错误: {magic[0]:X2} {magic[1]:X2}");
25: 
26:             var lenList = new List<byte>();
27:             while (true)
28:             {
29:                 byte[] b = new byte[1];
30:                 if (ReadExactly(stream, b, 1) != 1)
31:                     return null;
32:                 lenList.Add(b[0]);
33:                 if ((b[0] & 0x80) == 0) break;
34:             }
35:             long length = BytesToLength(lenList.ToArray());
36: 
37:             if (length == 0) return Array.Empty<byte>();
38:             byte[] payload = new byte[length];
39:             if (ReadExactly(stream, payload, (int)length) != length)
40:                 return null;
41:             return payload;
42:         }
43: 
44:         private static int ReadExactly(NetworkStream stream, byte[] buffer, int count)
45:         {
46:             int total = 0;
47:             while (total < count)
48:             {
49:                 // stream.Read 读的是字节不是位
50:                 int n = stream.Read(buffer, total, count - total);
51:                 if (n == 0) return total;
52:                 total += n;
53:             }
54:             //返回的是已经读取的字节数
55:             return total;
56:         }
57: 
58:         public static byte[] LengthToBytes(long length)
59:         {
60:             if (length == 0) return new byte[] { 0x00 };
61: 
62:             var bytes = new List<byte>();
63:             while (length > 0)
64:             {
65:                 bytes.Add((byte)(length & 0x7F));
66:                 length >>= 7;
67:             }
68:             bytes.Reverse();
69:             for (int i = 0; i < bytes.Count - 1; i++)
70:                 bytes[i] |= 0x80;
71:             return bytes.ToArray();
72:         }
73: 
74:         public static long BytesToLength(byte[] bytes)
75:         {
76:             long n = 0;
77:             for (int i = 0; i < bytes.Length; i++)
78:             {
79:                 n <<= 7;
80:                 n |= (long)(bytes[i] & 0x7F);
81:             }
82:             return n;
83:         }
84:     }
85: }

(End of file - total 85 lines)
</content>
```

7: namespace NetLab.Server

9:     public class EchoServer

14:         {
15:             _port = port;
16:         }
17: 
18:         public void Start()
19:         {
20:             TcpListener listener = new TcpListener(IPAddress.Any, _port);
21:             listener.Start();
22:             Console.WriteLine($"Echo 服务端已启动，监听 0.0.0.0:{_port}");
23:             Console.WriteLine("等待客户端连接...");
24: 
25:             while (true)
26:             {
27:                 TcpClient client = listener.AcceptTcpClient();
28:                 Console.WriteLine($"客户端已连接：{client.Client.RemoteEndPoint}");
29:                 Task.Run(() => HandleClient(client));
30:             }
31:         }
32: 
33:         private void HandleClient(TcpClient client)
34:         {
35:             try
36:             {
37:                 using NetworkStream stream = client.GetStream();
38: 
39:                 while (true)
40:                 {
41:                     byte[]? payload = FrameCodec.ReceiveFrame(stream);
42:                     if (payload == null)
43:                     {
44:                         Console.WriteLine($"客户端 {client.Client.RemoteEndPoint} 已断开");
45:                         break;
46:                     }
47:                     if (payload != null && payload.Length > 0 && payload[0] == 0xFF)
48:                     {
49:                         Console.WriteLine("收到心跳");
50:                         // 不回复或回复特定内容
51:                     }
52:                     else
53:                     {
54:                         string text = Encoding.UTF8.GetString(payload);
55:                         Console.WriteLine($"[{client.Client.RemoteEndPoint}] 收到帧：{payload.Length} 字节 → {text}");
56: 
57:                         // 业务层构造 ASDU → 转字节 → 传给传输层
58:                         IAsdu asdu = new BinaryAsdu(payload);
59:                         FrameCodec.SendFrame(stream, asdu.GetContent());
60:                         Console.WriteLine($"[{client.Client.RemoteEndPoint}] 回显 {payload.Length} 字节");
61:                     }
62:   
63:                 }
64:             }
65:             catch (Exception ex)
66:             {
67:                 Console.WriteLine($"处理客户端出错：{ex.Message}");
68:             }
69:             finally
70:             {
71:                 client.Close();
72:             }
73:         }
74:     }
75: }

(End of file - total 75 lines)

## Assistant (Build · DeepSeek V4 Pro · 8.1s)

_Thinking:_

Great, now I have the full picture. The user already extracted shared code into `Protocol/` (namespace `NetLab.Protocol`). They also added:
- `HealthbeatAsdu` (heartbeat msg with 0xFF)
- An extended EchoClient that sends 5 messages including a 5000-byte payload
- EchoServer has heartbeat detection

Now my plan:

1. Fix HeartbeatAsdu.cs namespace bug (`Protocol.Messages` → `NetLab.Protocol.Messages`)
2. Create `Protocol/Exchange/` directory
3. Create `Protocol/Exchange/IExchange.cs`
4. Create `Protocol/Exchange/StreamExchange.cs`
5. Add IExchange overloads to `Protocol/FrameCodec.cs`
6. Update `Server/EchoServer.cs` to use IExchange
7. Create `Client/Net.cs`
8. Update `Client/EchoClient.cs` to use IExchange + demonstrate Net.Send
9. Create docs

Let me also check the HeartbeatAsdu problem:
- Line 1: `using NetLab.Protocol.Messages;` - this is wrong, shouldn't be using its own namespace
- Line 8: `namespace Protocol.Messages` - should be `namespace NetLab.Protocol.Messages`
- The `IAsdu` reference will fail because `Protocol.Messages` is not `NetLab.Protocol.Messages`

Let me fix this and do everything in parallel.

For FrameCodec, I need to add:
- `using NetLab.Protocol.Exchange;`
- `SendFrame(IExchange exchange, byte[] payload)`
- `ReceiveFrame(IExchange exchange)`

The key difference from NetworkStream versions: IExchange.Send takes the full frame at once, and IExchange.ReadExactly does the loop internally.

For EchoServer, it will:
```csharp
using IExchange exchange = new StreamExchange(stream);
// then use FrameCodec.SendFrame(exchange, ...) and FrameCodec.ReceiveFrame(exchange)

ReadExactly(int count)\n        {\n            byte[] buffer = new byte[count];\n            int total = 0;\n            while (total < count)\n            {\n                int n = _stream.Read(buffer, total, count - total);\n                if (n == 0) return null;\n                total += n;\n            }\n            return buffer;\n        }\n\n        public void Close()\n        {\n            try { _stream.Close(); } catch { }\n        }\n\n        public void Dispose()\n        {\n            Close();\n        }\n    }\n}\n",

```json
{
  "content": "using System.Net.Sockets;\nusing NetLab.Protocol.Exchange;\n\nnamespace NetLab.Protocol\n{\n    public static class FrameCodec\n    {\n        private static readonly byte[] Magic = { 0xEB, 0x90 };\n\n        // ===== NetworkStream 版本（保留） =====\n\n        public static void SendFrame(NetworkStream stream, byte[] payload)\n        {\n            stream.Write(Magic, 0, 2);\n            byte[] lenBytes = LengthToBytes(payload.LongLength);\n            stream.Write(lenBytes, 0, lenBytes.Length);\n            stream.Write(payload, 0, payload.Length);\n            stream.Flush();\n        }\n\n        public static byte[]? ReceiveFrame(NetworkStream stream)\n        {\n            byte[] magic = new byte[2];\n            if (ReadExactly(stream, magic, 2) != 2)\n                return null;\n            if (magic[0] != 0xEB || magic[1] != 0x90)\n                throw new Exception($\"帧头错误: {magic[0]:X2} {magic[1]:X2}\");\n\n            return ReadPayload(stream);\n        }\n\n        // ===== IExchange 版本（Phase 2 新增） =====\n\n        public static void SendFrame(IExchange exchange, byte[] payload)\n        {\n            byte[] lenBytes = LengthToBytes(payload.LongLength);\n            byte[] frame = new byte[2 + lenBytes.Length + payload.Length];\n            Array.Copy(Magic, 0, frame, 0, 2);\n            Array.Copy(lenBytes, 0, frame, 2, lenBytes.Length);\n            Array.Copy(payload, 0, frame, 2 + lenBytes.Length, payload.Length);\n            exchange.Send(frame);\n        }\n\n        public static byte[]? ReceiveFrame(IExchange exchange)\n        {\n            byte[]? magic = exchange.ReadExactly(2);\n            if (magic == null) return null;\n            if (magic[0] != 0xEB || magic[1] != 0x90)\n                throw new Exception($\"帧头错误: {magic[0]:X2} {magic[1]:X2}\");\n\n            return ReadPayload(exchange);\n        }\n\n        // ===== 读载荷（内部，NetworkStream / IExchange 各一份） =====\n\n        private static byte[]? ReadPayload(NetworkStream stream)\n        {\n            var lenList = new List<byte>();\n            while (true)\n            {\n                byte[] b = new byte[1];\n                if (ReadExactly(stream, b, 1) != 1) return null;\n                lenList.Add(b[0]);\n                if ((b[0] & 0x80) == 0) break;\n            }\n            long length = BytesToLength(lenList.ToArray());\n            if (length == 0) return Array.Empty<byte>();\n            byte[] payload = new byte[length];\n            if (ReadExactly(stream, payload, (int)length) != length) return null;\n            return payload;\n        }\n\n        private static byte[]? ReadPayload(IExchange exchange)\n        {\n            var lenList = new List<byte>();\n            while (true)\n            {\n                byte[]? b = exchange.ReadExactly(1);\n                if (b == null) return null;\n                lenList.Add(b[0]);\n                if ((b[0] & 0x80) == 0) break;\n            }\n            long length = BytesToLength(lenList.ToArray());\n            if (length == 0) return Array.Empty<byte>();\n            if (length > int.MaxValue) throw new Exception($\"载荷过大: {length}\");\n            return exchange.ReadExactly((int)length);\n        }\n\n        // ===== 工具 =====\n\n        private static int ReadExactly(NetworkStream stream, byte[] buffer, int count)\n        {\n            int total = 0;\n            while (total < count)\n            {\n                int n = stream.Read(buffer, total, count - total);\n                if (n == 0) return total;\n                total += n;\n            }\n            return total;\n        }\n\n        public static byte[] LengthToBytes(long length)\n        {\n            if (length == 0) return new byte[] { 0x00 };\n            var bytes = new List<byte>();\n            while (length > 0)\n            {\n                bytes.Add((byte)(length & 0x7F));\n                length >>= 7;\n            }\n            bytes.Reverse();\n            for (int i = 0; i < bytes.Count - 1; i++)\n                bytes[i] |= 0x80;\n            return bytes.ToArray();\n        }\n\n        public static long BytesToLength(byte[] bytes)\n        {\n            long n = 0;\n            for (int i = 0; i < bytes.Length; i++)\n            {\n                n <<= 7;\n                n |= (long)(bytes[i] & 0x7F);\n            }\n            return n;\n        }\n    }\n}\n",
  "filePath": "D:\\code\\lab\\NetLab\\Protocol\\FrameCodec.cs"
}

**Input:**
```json
{
  "content": "# Phase 2.1 — IExchange 接口：传输层抽象\n\n> 目标：不再直接依赖 `NetworkStream`，用接口抽象掉底层读写方式。为后续加密切换打下基础。\n\n---\n\n## 1. 问题引入\n\n当前 EchoServer / EchoClient 直接操作 `NetworkStream`：\n\n```csharp\n// 问题：代码直接依赖 NetworkStream\nusing NetworkStream stream = client.GetStream();\nbyte[] payload = FrameCodec.ReceiveFrame(stream);   // stream 字面量\nFrameCodec.SendFrame(stream, payload);              // stream 字面量\n```\n\n三个问题：\n\n1. **无法替换**：如果将来换成 TLCP 加密（不走 `NetworkStream` 而走 `Ysh.Tlcp.TlcpClient`），所有调用的地方都得改\n2. **无法测试**：单元测试没法 mock 一个 `NetworkStream`（它依赖真实的 socket）\n3. **职责混合**：业务代码关心的是\"收一条消息/发一条消息\"，不应该知道底层是 `NetworkStream` 还是 `TlcpClient`\n\n---\n\n## 2. 方案：IExchange 接口\n\n定义一套方法签名，描述\"能收发字节、能关连接\"的抽象能力：\n\n```csharp\npublic interface IExchange : IDisposable\n{\n    void Send(byte[] data);              // 发字节\n    byte[]? ReadExactly(int count);      // 精确读满 count 字节，断开返回 null\n    void Close();                        // 关连接（Dispose 内部调 Close）\n    bool IsConnected { get; }            // 连接是否存活\n}\n```\n\n关键设计决策：\n\n| 决策 | 原因 |\n|------|------|\n| `ReadExactly(count)` 不是 `Read(buffer, offset, count)` | 协议层要\"读满指定字节\"，不要半包语义 |\n| 返回 `byte[]?`，null = 断开 | 调用方只需判空，不需要检查实际读了多少 |\n| 继承 `IDisposable` + 保留 `Close()` | `using` 能自动清理；`Close()` 可重复调用不报错 |\n\n---\n\n## 3. 实现：StreamExchange\n\n```csharp\npublic class StreamExchange : IExchange\n{\n    private readonly NetworkStream _stream;\n\n    public StreamExchange(NetworkStream stream)\n    {\n        _stream = stream;\n    }\n\n    public void Send(byte[] data)\n    {\n        _stream.Write(data, 0, data.Length);\n        _stream.Flush();\n    }\n\n    public byte[]? ReadExactly(int count)\n    {\n        byte[] buffer = new byte[count];\n        int total = 0;\n        while (total < count)\n        {\n            int n = _stream.Read(buffer, total, count - total);\n            if (n == 0) return null;   // 对端断开\n            total += n;\n        }\n        return buffer;\n    }\n\n    public bool IsConnected\n    {\n        get\n        {\n            try { return !(_socket.Poll(0, SelectMode.SelectRead) && _socket.Available == 0); }\n            catch { return false; }\n        }\n    }\n\n    public void Close() { try { _stream.Close(); } catch { } }\n    public void Dispose() => Close();\n}\n```\n\n注意：`ReadExactly` 内部做循环读，调用方（`FrameCodec`）不再自己处理半包问题。这是和原来 `FrameCodec.ReadExactly(NetworkStream stream, ...)` 的本质区别——原来循环读逻辑在 `FrameCodec` 里，现在移到 `IExchange` 实现里。\n\n---\n\n## 4. FrameCodec 加 IExchange 版本\n\n```csharp\n// ==== 新增 IExchange 版本 ====\n\npublic static void SendFrame(IExchange exchange, byte[] payload)\n{\n    byte[] lenBytes = LengthToBytes(payload.LongLength);\n    byte[] frame = new byte[2 + lenBytes.Length + payload.Length];\n    Array.Copy(Magic, 0, frame, 0, 2);\n    Array.Copy(lenBytes, 0, frame, 2, lenBytes.Length);\n    Array.Copy(payload, 0, frame, 2 + lenBytes.Length, payload.Length);\n    exchange.Send(frame);   // 一次 Send，发完整帧\n}\n\npublic static byte[]? ReceiveFrame(IExchange exchange)\n{\n    byte[]? magic = exchange.ReadExactly(2);\n    if (magic == null) return null;\n    // ... 逐字节读长度 → 精确读载荷 → return payload\n}\n```\n\n与 NetworkStream 版本的区别：\n\n| 维度 | NetworkStream 版本 | IExchange 版本 |\n|------|-------------------|---------------|\n| 发送 | 三次 `stream.Write`（帧头/长度/载荷） | 拼好整帧，一次 `exchange.Send` |\n| 接收 | 手动 `ReadExactly(stream, ...)` 循环 | `exchange.ReadExactly(count)` 一步到位 |\n| 用哪个 | 向后兼容旧代码 | **Phase 2 起推荐** |\n\n---\n\n## 5. 改造效果\n\n### 改造前（直接依赖 NetworkStream）\n\n```csharp\n// EchoServer\nusing NetworkStream stream = client.GetStream();\nbyte[] payload = FrameCodec.ReceiveFrame(stream);\nFrameCodec.SendFrame(stream, payload);\n\n// EchoClient\nusing NetworkStream stream = client.GetStream();\nFrameCodec.SendFrame(stream, Encoding.UTF8.GetBytes(\"AAAA\"));\nbyte[] response = FrameCodec.ReceiveFrame(stream);\n```\n\n### 改造后（通过 IExchange）\n\n```csharp\n// EchoServer\nusing IExchange exchange = new StreamExchange(client.GetStream());\nbyte[] payload = FrameCodec.ReceiveFrame(exchange);\nIAsdu asdu = new BinaryAsdu(payload);\nFrameCodec.SendFrame(exchange, asdu.GetContent());\n\n// EchoClient — 方式一：直接持 IExchange\nusing IExchange exchange = ...;\nFrameCodec.SendFrame(exchange, msg.GetContent());\nbyte[] response = FrameCodec.ReceiveFrame(exchange);\n\n// EchoClient — 方式二：通过 Net.Send（下一步学）\nbyte[] response = Net.Send(\"127.0.0.1\", 9000, asdu);\n```\n\n关键变化：EchoServer 和 EchoClient 不再 `using System.Net.Sockets;` 不需要知道底层是 TCP。只依赖 `IExchange`。\n\n---\n\n## 6. 对照 RemoteOps\n\n| NetLab | RemoteOps | 文件 |\n|--------|----------|------|\n| `IExchange` | `IExchange` | `services/YCYWDataExchange/.../Exchange/IExchange.cs` |\n| `StreamExchange` | `TCPClient` | `services/YCYWDataExchange/.../Exchange/TCPClient.cs` |\n| — | `TLCPClient` | `services/TLCPDataExchange/TLCPClient.cs`（下一版本 IExchange 实现） |\n\n> RemoteOps 里 `TCPClient` 这个名字容易误解——它不是 TcpClient 本身，而是包装了 TcpClient 的 IExchange 实现。NetLab 命名为 `StreamExchange` 更准确。\n\n---\n\n## 自检清单\n\n- [ ] `IExchange.ReadExactly(100)` 和 `NetworkStream.Read(buf, 0, 100)` 有什么区别？\n- [ ] 为什么 `FrameCodec` 同时保留 NetworkStream 和 IExchange 两套接口？\n- [ ] 如果将来要加 MockExchange（测试用），需要改 EchoServer 的代码吗？\n",
  "filePath": "D:\\code\\lab\\NetLab\\docs\\tutorials\\03-iexchange-interface.md"
}
```

**Output:**
```
Wrote file successfully.

**Tool: write**

**Input:**
```json
{
  "content": "# Phase 2.2 — 委托注入：明文/加密透明切换\n\n> 目标：通过一个静态委托，让全进程用一种统一的 IExchange 实现。为后续 TLCP 加密零改动替换打下基础。\n\n---\n\n## 1. 问题引入\n\n现在有了 `IExchange`，业务代码用 `IExchange` 收发。但创建连接时还是硬编码：\n\n```csharp\n// 硬编码：创建 StreamExchange\nTcpClient client = new TcpClient(\"127.0.0.1\", 9000);\nIExchange exchange = new StreamExchange(client.GetStream());\n```\n\n问题：如果将来有 20 处代码都创建连接，改加密时得改 20 处。而且每个调用方都要知道\"加密是用 TLCPClient 还是 TCPClient\"——这不是调用方该关心的。\n\n---\n\n## 2. 方案：静态委托作为全局工厂\n\n```csharp\npublic static class Net\n{\n    // 声明委托类型\n    public delegate IExchange CreateExchangeFunc(string ip, int port);\n\n    // 全局唯一的连接工厂，启动时赋值一次\n    public static CreateExchangeFunc? CreateExchange = null;\n\n    // 业务层唯一入口：发一个 ASDU，等一个响应\n    public static byte[]? Send(string ip, int port, IAsdu asdu)\n    {\n        using IExchange exchange = CreateExchange(ip, port);\n        FrameCodec.SendFrame(exchange, asdu.GetContent());\n        return FrameCodec.ReceiveFrame(exchange);\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### 启动时注册（一行切换）\n\n```csharp\n// 明文 TCP\nNet.CreateExchange = (ip, port) =>\n{\n    TcpClient client = new TcpClient(ip, port);\n    return new StreamExchange(client.GetStream());\n};\n\n// 将来：TLCP 加密（一行改掉，所有业务代码不动）\nNet.CreateExchange = (ip, port) =>\n{\n    // 1. TCP 连接\n    // 2. TLCP 握手\n    // 3. 返回用 TlcpClient 包装的 IExchange\n};\n```\n\n---\n\n## 3. 委托注入的核心价值\n\n```\n┌──────────────────────┐\n│  业务代码              │\n│  Net.Send(ip,port,asdu)│  ← 只管\"发消息收响应\"\n├──────────────────────┤\n│  Net.CreateExchange   │  ← 委托，启动时赋值一次\n│  (ip,port) => { ... } │\n├──────────────────────┤\n│  具体实现              │\n│  StreamExchange /     │\n│  将来: TLCPExchange   │\n└──────────────────────┘\n```\n\n编译时：`Net.Send` 只依赖 `IExchange` 接口，不依赖任何具体实现。\n运行时：通过 `Net.CreateExchange` 委托切换到具体实现。\n\nRemoteOps 里正是用这套机制实现了全站透明加密。\n\n---\n\n## 4. 使用方式\n\n### 方式一：长连接复用（多个请求-响应在同一连接上）\n\n```csharp\nNet.CreateExchange = (ip, port) => { ... };\n\nusing IExchange exchange = Net.CreateExchange(\"127.0.0.1\", 9000);\nfor (int i = 0; i < 3; i++)\n{\n    FrameCodec.SendFrame(exchange, msg.GetContent());\n    byte[] response = FrameCodec.ReceiveFrame(exchange);\n}\n```\n\n### 方式二：短连接每次新建（一个请求-响应建一次连接）\n\n```csharp\nNet.CreateExchange = (ip, port) => { ... };\n\nbyte[]? response = Net.Send(\"127.0.0.1\", 9000, asdu);\n// 内部：CreateExchange → SendFrame → ReceiveFrame → Dispose\n```\n\n方式二的代价：每次请求都新建 TCP 连接（三次握手开销）。Phase 3（连接池）会解决这个问题。\n\n---\n\n## 5. 和 RemoteOps Net.cs 的对应关系\n\nRemoteOps 的 `Helper/Net.cs` 同时包含了三件事：\n\n```csharp\n// RemoteOps Net.cs（真实代码简化）：\npublic static byte[] InternalSend(string ip, int port, IASDU asdu)\n{\n    using Extend<IExchange> ec = UseClient(ip, port);  // ← 连接池（Phase 3）\n    //        ↑ UseClient 内部调 CreateClient(ip, port)  ← 委托注入（Phase 2.2）\n    Net.Send(ec.Src, asdu);                             // ← 帧协议（Phase 1.1）\n    byte[] rResponse = APDU.Read(ec.Src);\n    return rResponse;\n}\n```\n\n| NetLab 教学 | RemoteOps 生产 | 混在一起的问题 |\n|------------|---------------|--------------|\n| `Phase 1.1 FrameCodec` | `APDU.WriteTo/Read` | Net.cs 里还塞了变长编码 |\n| `Phase 2.1 IExchange` | `IExchange.cs` | 干净 |\n| `Phase 2.2 Client.Net.cs` 委托 | `Net.CreateClient 委托` | 和连接池写在同一文件同一方法里 |\n| `Phase 3 连接池`（下一步） | `Net.UseClient/InternalSend` | 同上 |\n\n---\n\n## 6. 动手练习\n\n### 练习 1：观察 IsConnected\n\n在 `EchoClient.RunTest()` 里，发送消息前后打印 `exchange.IsConnected`。\n\n### 练习 2：自己写一个 MockExchange\n\n```csharp\npublic class MockExchange : IExchange\n{\n    private readonly byte[] _response;\n    public MockExchange(byte[] response) { _response = response; }\n\n    public void Send(byte[] data) { /* 不真发 */ }\n    public byte[]? ReadExactly(int count) => _response;\n    public void Close() { }\n    public void Dispose() { }\n    public bool IsConnected => true;\n}\n```\n\n然后注册到 `Net.CreateExchange`，验证业务代码不用改就能跑。\n\n### 练习 3：跟踪 ReadExactly 的调用链\n\n从 `EchoServer.HandleClient` 开始 → `FrameCodec.ReceiveFrame(exchange)` → `exchange.ReadExactly(2)` → `StreamExchange.ReadExactly` 内部循环。用断点或 Console.WriteLine 跟踪每一步。\n\n---\n\n## 7. 对照 RemoteOps\n\n| NetLab | RemoteOps | 备注 |\n|--------|----------|------|\n| `Client.Net.cs` | `Helper.Net.cs` | 教学只含委托 + Send；生产混杂了连接池 + 变长编码 |\n| `Net.CreateExchange` | `Net.CreateClient` | 同名不同实现，机制一致 |\n| `Net.CreateExchangeFunc` | `Net.CreateClientFunc` | 委托类型 |\n| `Net.Send(ip, port, asdu)` | `Net.InternalSend(ip, port, asdu)` | 教学版无连接池 |\n\n---\n\n## Phase 2 总结\n\n```\nPhase 2.1: IExchange 接口\n  业务代码不再直接依赖 NetworkStream\n  → StreamExchange 包装 NetworkStream\n  → FrameCodec 加 IExchange 版本重载\n\nPhase 2.2: 委托注入\n  创建连接的方式由 Net.CreateExchange 委托决定\n  → 启动时注册一次，全进程统一\n  → 明文/加密切换只需改一行\n```\n\n下一阶段（Phase 3）：连接池。解决 `Net.Send` 每次新建连接的开销。\n",
  "filePath": "D:\\code\\lab\\NetLab\\docs\\tutorials\\04-delegate-injection.md"

## Phase 2 交付总结

### 新增

| 文件 | 说明 |
|------|------|
| `Protocol/Exchange/IExchange.cs` | 接口：Send / ReadExactly / Close / IsConnected |
| `Protocol/Exchange/StreamExchange.cs` | NetworkStream 包装实现 |
| `Client/Net.cs` | 委托 `CreateExchange` + `Send(ip, port, asdu)` |
| `docs/tutorials/03-iexchange-interface.md` | Phase 2.1 教学文档 |
| `docs/tutorials/04-delegate-injection.md` | Phase 2.2 教学文档 |

### 修改

| 文件 | 改动 |
|------|------|
| `Protocol/FrameCodec.cs` | 加 `SendFrame(IExchange, byte[])` / `ReceiveFrame(IExchange)` |
| `Protocol/Messages/HealthbeatAsdu.cs` | 修复命名空间 bug |
| `Server/EchoServer.cs` | 改用 `IExchange`（`StreamExchange` 包装） |
| `Client/EchoClient.cs` | 改用 `IExchange` + `Net`；新增 `RunSingleTest()` |
| `docs/README.md` | Phase 2 拆分为 2.1 + 2.2 |

### 删除

| 项 | 说明 |
|------|------|
| `NetLab.Common/` | 冗余，已并入 `Protocol/` |

---

### 和 RemoteOps 的映射

```
NetLab                          RemoteOps
────────────────────────        ────────────────────────
Protocol/Exchange/IExchange →   IExchange.cs（干净对应）
Protocol/Exchange/StreamExchange →  TCPClient.cs（名字不同，本质相同）
Client/Net.cs 委托 + Send   →   Net.cs 委托 + InternalSend
                                  ↑ RemoteOps 混入了连接池 + 变长编码
FrameCodec.SendFrame(exchange) →  APDU.WriteTo(exchange)
```

Phase 3 预告：连接池 —— 解决 `Net.Send` 每次新建连接的开销。

**Output:**
```
<path>D:\code\lab\NetLab\docs\tutorials\笔记.md</path>
<type>file</type>
<content>
1: 变长长度编码可以理解成“128 进制”的长度表示。每个长度字节有 8 位，但最高位不用来表示数值，而是作为“后面是否还有长度字节”的标志；只有低 7 位参与计算。所以每多一个长度字节，就多 7 位表示能力。比如 300 可拆成 `[2,44]`，即 `2×128+44`，传输时变成 `[0x82,0x2C]`：`0x82` 表示数值 2 且后面还有，`0x2C` 表示数值 44 且长度结束。
2: 
3: 
4: 一个字节代表128 比如300 就是 第一个字节2 代表2\*128  第二个字节代表个位就是300%128的余数
5: 
6: 以首位比特判断变长后续还有无表示长度的字节 1 代表有 0代表没有
7: 
8: 
9: 传输帧只要字节流 所有的业务层主动向传输帧接口靠拢，为了能够让各个协议都支持 所以使用了IAsdu 接口来规范和限制这一约束必须实现。
10: 
11: `NetworkStream.Read(...)` 每读走几个**字节**，这几个字节就从 TCP 接收缓冲里被“消费掉”了。下一次 `Read` 会从后面的数据继续读。
12: 
13: TCP 保证字节流可靠、有序、不丢、不乱序；但不保证一次 `Read` 就把你想要的字节数全部给你。
14: 
15: 
16: `FrameCodec + Exchange` 抽象的是“面向业务消息的可靠帧收发能力”，它把底层 TCP 字节流包装成一条条可识别的业务消息。
17: 
18: 
19: IAsdu
20: = 我要发什么业务内容
21: 
22: FrameCodec
23: = 业务内容怎么包装成一帧、怎么从一帧里拆出来
24: 
25: Exchange
26: = 这一帧字节通过什么通道发出去、怎么读回来
27: 
28: Exchange + FrameCodec = MessageTransport，消息传输能力
29: 
30: 业务代码
31: ↓
32: MessageTransport：发送一条业务消息 / 接收一条业务消息
33: ↓
34: FrameCodec：把消息变成帧，或从帧里拆消息
35: ↓
36: Exchange：把帧字节真正发出去 / 读回来
37: ↓
38: TCP / TLCP / Mock
39: 
40: 
41: 业务代码调用 `FrameCodec` 发一帧；`FrameCodec` 不亲自联网，只调用 `Exchange` 把这一帧字节发出去。
42: 
43: 
44: `Net` 既管理连接创建方式，也在 `FrameCodec` 之上提供了一层“发送业务消息并接收响应”的封装。调用方只关心发什么、发到哪、收到什么，不关心帧协议和底层通道。

(End of file - total 44 lines)
</content>
```

## Phase 3 计划 — 连接池

### 问题

当前 `Net.Send()` 每次新建 TCP 连接：

```csharp
public static byte[]? Send(string ip, int port, IAsdu asdu)
{
    using IExchange exchange = CreateExchange(ip, port);  // 每次 new TcpClient + 三次握手
    FrameCodec.SendFrame(exchange, asdu.GetContent());
    return FrameCodec.ReceiveFrame(exchange);
}  // using 结束 → exchange.Dispose() → Close() → 四次挥手
```

代价：每个请求 1 次握手 + 1 次挥手。主站每秒几十个请求时开销不可接受。

### 方案

`ConcurrentDictionary<string, List<Extend<IExchange>>>`

- key = `"ip:port"`
- value = 该目标的所有空闲连接列表
- `Extend<IExchange>`：包装 `IExchange` + `IsUsing` 标记
- `using (Extend<IExchange> ec = UseClient(ip, port))` → 自动归还

### 教学拆法（和 RemoteOps 的区别）

| RemoteOps Net.cs | NetLab 教学 |
|-----------------|------------|
| `UseClient` 里：委托创建 + 协商帧 + 返回 | Phase 2 委托已在 `Net.cs` 里，Phase 3 只讲池 |
| `InternalSend` 里：取连接 + 发送 + 等回包 | Phase 3 改造 `Net.Send` 加池 |
| 变长编码也在 Net.cs | Phase 1 已拆到 FrameCodec |

### 产出清单

| # | 文件 | 动作 |
|---|------|------|
| 1 | `Client/ConnectionPool.cs` | 新建 — ConcurrentDictionary 池 + Extend\<T\> + UseClient |
| 2 | `Client/Net.cs` | 改造 — `Send` 内部改为 `UseClient` 取连接 |
| 3 | `docs/tutorials/05-connection-pool.md` | 新建 |
| 4 | `docs/README.md` | 更新 |

4 项，结构简单。等你的确认。

---

## User

这个计划主线没问题，可以进 Phase 3。

但我建议执行前只补一个关键约束：

> `ConcurrentDictionary` 只保证字典本身线程安全，不保证里面的 `List<Extend<IExchange>>` 线程安全。

也就是说这个结构：

```csharp
ConcurrentDictionary<string, List<Extend<IExchange>>>
```

外层 `key -> value` 安全，但多个线程同时操作同一个 `List` 时，还是可能出问题。

所以教学版可以二选一：

```text
方案 A：保留 List，但每个 key 对应的 List 操作都加 lock
方案 B：直接用 ConcurrentBag / ConcurrentQueue，少讲锁
```

如果是为了对照 RemoteOps，我建议用 **方案 A**：

```csharp
private class PoolBucket
{
    public readonly object Lock = new object();
    public readonly List<Extend<IExchange>> Items = new();
}
```

然后结构变成：

```csharp
ConcurrentDictionary<string, PoolBucket>
```

这样教学上更清楚：

```text
ConcurrentDictionary 负责多目标 ip:port 的并发访问
lock 负责单个连接池列表的并发访问
```

另外 `Extend<IExchange>` 这个名字偏生产代码风格，教学里可以叫：

```text
PooledExchange
或
ExchangeLease
```

更直观：

> 从池里“借出”一个连接，用完 Dispose 自动归还。

结论：**计划可以执行，但连接池容器建议从 `ConcurrentDictionary<string, List<...>>` 改成 `ConcurrentDictionary<string, PoolBucket>`，避免把线程安全问题讲歪。** 
选择方案A吧

_Thinking:_

2. `Client/Net.cs` - modify Send to use UseClient
3. `docs/tutorials/05-connection-pool.md`

Let me think about the Extend<T> naming. The user suggests `PooledExchange` or `ExchangeLease`. Let me think about which is clearer:

- `Extend<IExchange>` - RemoteOps name, confusing (Extend means "extend" but it's a wrapper)
- `PooledExchange` - clear: an exchange from the pool
- `ExchangeLease` - emphasizes the borrow/return model

I'll use `ExchangeLease` - it's the most descriptive. "租约" concept is intuitive.

Let me layout the ConnectionPool.cs design:

```csharp
namespace NetLab.Client
{
    // 连接租约：包装 IExchange + IsUsing 标记，Dispose 归还
    public class ExchangeLease : IDisposable
    {
        private readonly ConnectionPool _pool;
        private readonly string _key;
        public IExchange Exchange { get; }
        public bool IsUsing { get; private set; }

        internal ExchangeLease(ConnectionPool pool, string key, IExchange exchange)
        {
            _pool = pool;
            _key = key;
            Exchange = exchange;
            IsUsing = true;
        }

        public void Dispose()
        {
            IsUsing = false;  // 归还，不断开连接
        }
    }

    // 单个目标地址的连接桶
    internal class PoolBucket
    {
        public readonly object Lock = new();
        public readonly List<ExchangeLease> Items = new();
    }

    public class ConnectionPool
    {
        private readonly ConcurrentDictionary<string, PoolBucket> _buckets = new();
        private readonly Net.CreateExchangeFunc _factory;

        public ConnectionPool(Net.CreateExchangeFunc factory)
        {
            _factory = factory;
        }

        public ExchangeLease? UseClient(string ip, int port)
        {
            string key = $"{ip}:{port}";
            PoolBucket bucket = _buckets.GetOrAdd(key, _ => new PoolBucket());

            lock (bucket.Lock)
            {
                // 反向遍历，找空闲且存活的连接
                for (int i = bucket.Items.Count - 1; i >= 0; i--)
                {
                    if (bucket.Items[i].IsUsing) continue;
                    if (bucket.Items[i].Exchange.IsConnected)
                    {
                        bucket.Items[i].IsUsing = true;
                        return bucket.Items[i];
                    }
                    bucket.Items.RemoveAt(i);
                }

                // 无可用连接 → 新建
                IExchange exchange = _factory(ip, port);
                if (exchange == null) return null;

                var lease = new ExchangeLease(this, key, exchange);
                bucket.Items.Add(lease);
                return lease;
            }
        }
    }
}
```

Wait, I need to think about the `Dispose` of ExchangeLease. Currently it just sets `IsUsing = false`. But what about actually closing the connection? The pool should eventually clean up stale connections, but for simplicity:

- `ExchangeLease.Dispose()` just marks `IsUsing = false` (returns to pool)
- Dead connections are removed during `UseClient` when they fail `IsConnected` check

This matches RemoteOps' `Extend<T>.Dispose()` which also just sets `isUsing = false`.

Now for Net.cs modification:

```csharp
public static class Net
{
    public delegate IExchange CreateExchangeFunc(string ip, int port);
    public static CreateExchangeFunc? CreateExchange = null;

    private static ConnectionPool? _pool;

    public static byte[]? Send(string ip, int port, IAsdu asdu)
    {
        if (_pool == null)
            _pool = new ConnectionPool(CreateExchange!);

        using ExchangeLease lease = _pool.UseClient(ip, port);
        if (lease == null) return null;

        FrameCodec.SendFrame(lease.Exchange, asdu.GetContent());
        return FrameCodec.ReceiveFrame(lease.Exchange);
    }
}
```

But wait - `ExchangeLease.Dispose()` needs to also do the `IsUsing = false` in `PoolBucket`. The connection pool owns the leases. But with `using ExchangeLease lease = ...`, when the using block ends, `lease.Dispose()` is called, which sets `IsUsing = false`. The `_pool` reference isn't strictly needed in `ExchangeLease.Dispose()` if all it does is set a flag.

Actually, let me simplify: `ExchangeLease.Dispose()` just sets `IsUsing = false`. That's exactly what RemoteOps does.

Let me finalize the plan and present it.

For the document, I should emphasize:
1. Problem: each Net.Send creates new TCP connection
2. Solution: pool connections by ip:port
3. Key classes: ExchangeLease, PoolBucket, ConnectionPool
4. Thread safety: ConcurrentDictionary for multi-target, lock for single-target list
5. Integration: Net.Send uses UseClient instead of direct CreateExchange
6. Mapping to RemoteOps (Net.UseClient, Extend<T>, InternalSend)

Let me present the final plan.

好，方案 A 确认。下面是最终执行稿：

---

## Phase 3 执行计划

### 核心数据结构

```
ConcurrentDictionary<string, PoolBucket>
    key = "127.0.0.1:9000"
    value = PoolBucket { Lock, Items: List<ExchangeLease> }

ConcurrentDictionary — 多目标 ip:port 并发安全
lock(bucket.Lock)    — 单目标连接列表并发安全
```

### ExchangeLease（对应 RemoteOps 的 Extend\<T\>）

```csharp
public class ExchangeLease : IDisposable
{
    public IExchange Exchange { get; }
    public bool IsUsing { get; internal set; }

    public void Dispose()
    {
        IsUsing = false;  // 归还池，不关连接
    }
}
```

### PoolBucket

```csharp
internal class PoolBucket
{
    public readonly object Lock = new();
    public readonly List<ExchangeLease> Items = new();
}
```

### ConnectionPool.UseClient 核心逻辑

```
1. GetOrAdd bucket by "ip:port"
2. lock(bucket.Lock)
3. 反向遍历 Items，找 IsUsing==false 且 IsConnected==true 的连接
   → 找到：标记 IsUsing=true，返回
   → 连接已死：RemoveAt，继续找
4. 没找到：调 _factory(ip, port) 新建 → 包成 ExchangeLease → Add → 返回
```

### 产出清单

| # | 文件 | 动作 |
|---|------|------|
| 1 | `Client/ConnectionPool.cs` | 新建 — `ExchangeLease` + `PoolBucket` + `ConnectionPool` |
| 2 | `Client/Net.cs` | 改造 — `Send` 改为 `_pool.UseClient` 取连接 |
| 3 | `docs/tutorials/05-connection-pool.md` | 新建 |
| 4 | `docs/README.md` | Phase 3 状态更新 |

### Net.cs 改造前后对比

```csharp
// 改造前
public static byte[]? Send(string ip, int port, IAsdu asdu)
{
    using IExchange exchange = CreateExchange(ip, port);  // 每次新建
    FrameCodec.SendFrame(exchange, asdu.GetContent());
    return FrameCodec.ReceiveFrame(exchange);
}

// 改造后
private static ConnectionPool? _pool;

public static byte[]? Send(string ip, int port, IAsdu asdu)
{
    _pool ??= new ConnectionPool(CreateExchange!);
    using ExchangeLease lease = _pool.UseClient(ip, port);  // 池化
    if (lease == null) return null;
    FrameCodec.SendFrame(lease.Exchange, asdu.GetContent());
    return FrameCodec.ReceiveFrame(lease.Exchange);
}
```

### RemoteOps 对照

| NetLab | RemoteOps |
|--------|----------|
| `ExchangeLease` | `Extend<IExchange>` (`Helper/Extend.cs`) |
| `ConnectionPool` | `Net.cs:115` `ConcurrentDictionary<string, List<Extend<IExchange>>>` |
| `UseClient(ip, port)` | `Net.UseClient(ip, port)` |
| `Send(ip, port, asdu)` | `Net.InternalSend(ip, port, asdu)` |

### 文档要点

1. 问题：Stopwatch 对比——10 次请求，新建 vs 池化耗时差
2. 结构：`ExchangeLease` 租约模式 → `PoolBucket` 锁粒度 → `ConnectionPool` 整体
3. 线程安全：ConcurrentDictionary 干嘛的、lock 干嘛的，各管什么
4. 与 Phase 2 的关系：Phase 2 的委托决定"怎么建"，Phase 3 的池决定"什么时候建/什么时候复用"
5. 练习：并发发 100 个请求，统计实际 TCP 连接数

---

Let me start by reading the current `Client/Net.cs` to know exactly what to modify.

Actually, I already know the content from earlier. Let me just write everything.

For ConnectionPool.cs:
```csharp
using System.Collections.Concurrent;
using NetLab.Protocol.Exchange;

namespace NetLab.Client
{
    public class ExchangeLease : IDisposable
    {
        public IExchange Exchange { get; }
        public bool IsUsing { get; internal set; }

        public ExchangeLease(IExchange exchange)
        {
            Exchange = exchange;
            IsUsing = true;
        }

        public void Dispose()
        {
            IsUsing = false;  // 归还池，不关连接
        }
    }

    internal class PoolBucket
    {
        public readonly object Lock = new();
        public readonly List<ExchangeLease> Items = new();
    }

    public class ConnectionPool
    {
        private readonly Net.CreateExchangeFunc _factory;
        private readonly ConcurrentDictionary<string, PoolBucket> _buckets = new();

        public ConnectionPool(Net.CreateExchangeFunc factory)
        {
            _factory = factory;
        }

        public ExchangeLease? UseClient(string ip, int port)
        {
            string key = $"{ip}:{port}";
            PoolBucket bucket = _buckets.GetOrAdd(key, _ => new PoolBucket());

            lock (bucket.Lock)
            {
                // 反向遍历，找空闲且存活的连接
                for (int i = bucket.Items.Count - 1; i >= 0; i--)
                {
                    ExchangeLease lease = bucket.Items[i];
                    if (lease.IsUsing) continue;

                    if (lease.Exchange.IsConnected)
                    {
                        lease.IsUsing = true;
                        return lease;
                    }

                    // 连接已死，移除
                    lease.Exchange.Close();
                    bucket.Items.RemoveAt(i);
                }

                // 没有可用连接，新建
                IExchange exchange = _factory(ip, port);
                if (exchange == null) return null;

                ExchangeLease newLease = new ExchangeLease(exchange);
                bucket.Items.Add(newLease);
                return newLease;
            }
        }
    }
}
```

Wait, there's a subtle issue. `ExchangeLease.Dispose()` sets `IsUsing = false` but doesn't call `exchange.Close()`. That's the whole point of the pool - the connection stays alive. But the `using` pattern will call Dispose when done, which returns it to the pool.

But there's a problem: what if `ExchangeLease.Dispose()` is called AND we also need to make sure the underlying `IExchange` is eventually disposed? The pool is responsible for cleaning up dead connections.

Let me think about this more carefully...

In RemoteOps, `Extend<T>.Dispose()` only sets `isUsing = false`. The actual connection close happens when:
1. A new request finds the connection is dead during pool scan (calls Close)
2. Or when the process shuts down

For NetLab, I should follow the same pattern. The `ExchangeLease.Dispose()` just returns to pool. The pool itself handles cleanup when connections die.

For `Net.Send`, the using pattern is:
```csharp
using ExchangeLease lease = _pool.UseClient(ip, port);
// ... use lease.Exchange ...
// Dispose called here → IsUsing = false → returned to pool
```

This is correct.

Now for `Net.cs` update:

```csharp
using NetLab.Protocol;
using NetLab.Protocol.Exchange;
using NetLab.Protocol.Messages;

namespace NetLab.Client
{
    public static class Net
    {
        public delegate IExchange CreateExchangeFunc(string ip, int port);

        public static CreateExchangeFunc? CreateExchange = null;

        private static ConnectionPool? _pool;

        public static byte[]? Send(string ip, int port, IAsdu asdu)
        {
            if (CreateExchange == null)
                throw new InvalidOperationException("CreateExchange 未注册。");

            _pool ??= new ConnectionPool(CreateExchange);

            using ExchangeLease lease = _pool.UseClient(ip, port);
            if (lease == null) return null;

            FrameCodec.SendFrame(lease.Exchange, asdu.GetContent());
            return FrameCodec.ReceiveFrame(lease.Exchange);
        }
    }
}
```

Wait, but there's a concern: the `Send` method is synchronous and blocking. If two threads call `Send` simultaneously to the same ip:port, they'll each get a different lease (if available) or one will create a new one while the other waits on the lock. This matches RemoteOps behavior.

But wait - in the current design, `Send` does `SendFrame` then `ReceiveFrame` on the same connection. During `ReceiveFrame`, is the connection blocked? Yes, it's blocked reading. But since `ExchangeLease` is marked `IsUsing = true` during this time, other threads won't get this connection. They'll either find another idle one or create a new one.

This is the correct behavior.

Now let me think about the `Net.cs` delegate type. Currently `CreateExchangeFunc` is declared inside `Net`. And `ConnectionPool` takes `Net.CreateExchangeFunc`. But since `ConnectionPool` is in the same namespace (`NetLab.Client`) and `CreateExchangeFunc` is a nested type of `Net`, I need to reference it as `Net.CreateExchangeFunc`.

Let me make sure the using in ConnectionPool.cs is correct. I'll use `using NetLab.Protocol.Exchange;` for IExchange, and reference `Net.CreateExchangeFunc` as the delegate type since ConnectionPool is in the same namespace.

Actually, wait. Let me re-read the current Net.cs. It's at `Client/Net.cs` and the namespace is `NetLab.Client`. The delegate is `public delegate IExchange CreateExchangeFunc(string ip, int port);` inside `Net` class.

So `ConnectionPool` needs to use `Net.CreateExchangeFunc`. Since both are in `NetLab.Client` namespace, I can use `Net.CreateExchangeFunc` directly.

Let me also think about the document content for 05-connection-pool.md.

Key points:
1. Problem: measuring overhead of creating new connections
2. Solution: pool + lease pattern
3. ExchangeLease: IDisposable pattern for "return to pool"
4. PoolBucket: lock granularity
5. ConcurrentDictionary: why not just Dictionary + lock?
6. Thread safety analysis
7. Code walkthrough
8. Exercise: 100 concurrent requests, count actual TCP connections
9. RemoteOps mapping

Now let me also think about the EchoClient. Should it be updated to use the pool? The EchoClient currently uses `IExchange` directly (long connection, multiple messages). The pool is for `Net.Send` (short connection, one request). The EchoClient demonstrates the long-connection pattern which is separate from the pooled short-connection pattern. I'll leave EchoClient as-is and just modify `Net.cs` to use the pool for `Net.Send`.

Actually, looking at the current EchoClient code:
```csharp
using IExchange exchange = Net.CreateExchange(_host, _port);
```

This still creates a new connection, not using the pool. But that's fine - the pool is for `Net.Send`, not for raw `Net.CreateExchange` usage. The `Net.Send` wrapper is the pooled convenience method.

Wait, but should `Net.CreateExchange` go through the pool? In RemoteOps, `Net.CreateClient` is the factory delegate, and `Net.UseClient` uses it to create new connections for the pool. Direct calls to `CreateClient` bypass the pool.

For NetLab, I'll keep:
- `Net.CreateExchange` → factory delegate (unchanged)
- `Net.Send` → convenience method (now pooled)
- Direct `CreateExchange` calls → bypass pool (for long-connection use cases)

This is consistent with the RemoteOps design.

For the README.md update, I need to update the Phase 3 section to reflect completion.

  "content": "using System.Collections.Concurrent;\nusing NetLab.Protocol.Exchange;\n\nnamespace NetLab.Client\n{\n    public class ExchangeLease : IDisposable\n    {\n        public IExchange Exchange { get; }\n        public bool IsUsing { get; internal set; }\n\n        public ExchangeLease(IExchange exchange)\n        {\n            Exchange = exchange;\n            IsUsing = true;\n        }\n\n        public void Dispose()\n        {\n            IsUsing = false;\n        }\n    }\n\n    internal class PoolBucket\n    {\n        public readonly object Lock = new();\n        public readonly List<ExchangeLease> Items = new();\n    }\n\n    public class ConnectionPool\n    {\n        private readonly Net.CreateExchangeFunc _factory;\n        private readonly ConcurrentDictionary<string, PoolBucket> _buckets = new();\n\n        public ConnectionPool(Net.CreateExchangeFunc factory)\n        {\n            _factory = factory;\n        }\n\n        public ExchangeLease? UseClient(string ip, int port)\n        {\n            string key = $\"{ip}:{port}\";\n            PoolBucket bucket = _buckets.GetOrAdd(key, _ => new PoolBucket());\n\n            lock (bucket.Lock)\n            {\n                for (int i = bucket.Items.Count - 1; i >= 0; i--)\n                {\n                    ExchangeLease lease = bucket.Items[i];\n                    if (lease.IsUsing) continue;\n\n                    if (lease.Exchange.IsConnected)\n                    {\n                        lease.IsUsing = true;\n                        return lease;\n                    }\n\n                    lease.Exchange.Close();\n                    bucket.Items.RemoveAt(i);\n                }\n\n                IExchange exchange = _factory(ip, port);\n                if (exchange == null) return null;\n\n                ExchangeLease newLease = new ExchangeLease(exchange);\n                bucket.Items.Add(newLease);\n                return newLease;\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n",
  "filePath": "D:\\code\\lab\\NetLab\\Client\\ConnectionPool.cs"
}

**Tool: write**

**Input:**
```json
{
  "content": "# Phase 3 — 连接池：连接复用\n\n> 目标：`Net.Send` 不再每次新建 TCP 连接，用连接池复用。理解线程安全的租约模式。\n\n---\n\n## 1. 问题引入\n\nPhase 2 的 `Net.Send` 每次调用都新建 TCP：\n\n```csharp\npublic static byte[]? Send(string ip, int port, IAsdu asdu)\n{\n    using IExchange exchange = CreateExchange(ip, port);  // 三次握手\n    FrameCodec.SendFrame(exchange, asdu.GetContent());\n    return FrameCodec.ReceiveFrame(exchange);\n}   // using 结束 → Dispose → Close → 四次挥手\n```\n\n每个请求一次握手 + 一次挥手。主站每秒几十个请求时，开销不可接受。\n\n---\n\n## 2. 方案：连接池 + 租约模式\n\n核心思想：**用完不关，放回池里，下次复用。**\n\n```\n┌──────────────────────┐\n│  Net.Send(ip,port,asdu)│\n│    ↓                   │\n│  _pool.UseClient(...)  │  ← 从池里借\n│    ↓                   │\n│  SendFrame / ReceiveFrame\n│    ↓                   │\n│  lease.Dispose()       │  ← IsUsing = false（归还）\n└──────────────────────┘\n```\n\n### 数据结构\n\n```\nConcurrentDictionary<string, PoolBucket>\n     ↑                        ↑\n  key = \"127.0.0.1:9000\"    每个 ip:port 一个桶\n                             PoolBucket {\n                                 Lock (锁),\n                                 Items: List<ExchangeLease>\n                             }\n\nExchangeLease {\n    Exchange: IExchange,\n    IsUsing: bool           ← true = 被借出, false = 空闲\n}\n```\n\n### 线程安全分工\n\n| 层级 | 用什么保护 | 保护什么 |\n|------|-----------|---------|\n| 外层 | `ConcurrentDictionary` | 多 ip:port 目标并发访问 |\n| 内层 | `lock(bucket.Lock)` | 同一个 ip:port 的连接列表操作 |\n\n只用 `ConcurrentDictionary` 不够——它只保证 key-value 操作原子，不保证 List 的并发安全。双层保护各管各的。\n\n---\n\n## 3. 租约模式（ExchangeLease）\n\n```csharp\npublic class ExchangeLease : IDisposable\n{\n    public IExchange Exchange { get; }\n    public bool IsUsing { get; internal set; }\n\n    public ExchangeLease(IExchange exchange)\n    {\n        Exchange = exchange;\n        IsUsing = true;\n    }\n\n    public void Dispose()\n    {\n        IsUsing = false;   // 归还池，不关连接！\n    }\n}\n```\n\n关键：`Dispose()` 不调用 `exchange.Close()`。连接保持 ESTABLISHED，下次可以复用。\n\n配合 `using` 语法：\n\n```csharp\nusing ExchangeLease lease = pool.UseClient(ip, port);\n// 用 lease.Exchange 收发...\n// using 结束 → lease.Dispose() → IsUsing = false → 归还\n```\n\n---\n\n## 4. UseClient 核心逻辑\n\n```csharp\npublic ExchangeLease? UseClient(string ip, int port)\n{\n    string key = $\"{ip}:{port}\";\n    PoolBucket bucket = _buckets.GetOrAdd(key, _ => new PoolBucket());\n\n    lock (bucket.Lock)\n    {\n        // 步骤 1：反向遍历，找空闲且存活的连接\n        for (int i = bucket.Items.Count - 1; i >= 0; i--)\n        {\n            ExchangeLease lease = bucket.Items[i];\n            if (lease.IsUsing) continue;         // 正被别的线程用着\n\n            if (lease.Exchange.IsConnected)      // 连接还活着\n            {\n                lease.IsUsing = true;\n                return lease;\n            }\n\n            lease.Exchange.Close();              // 连接已死，清理\n            bucket.Items.RemoveAt(i);\n        }\n\n        // 步骤 2：没有可用连接，新建\n        IExchange exchange = _factory(ip, port);\n        if (exchange == null) return null;\n\n        ExchangeLease newLease = new ExchangeLease(exchange);\n        bucket.Items.Add(newLease);\n        return newLease;\n    }\n}\n```\n\n细节说明：\n\n| 细节 | 原因 |\n|------|------|\n| 反向遍历 | RemoveAt 时正序会导致索引错位 |\n| `IsConnected` 检查 | TCP 连接可能被对端关闭（FIN），不能复用一个死连接 |\n| 死连接先 `Close()` 再 `RemoveAt` | 确保 socket 资源释放 |\n| `lock` 包住整个查找+新建 | 防止两个线程同时发现没可用连接，同时新建两个 |\n\n---\n\n## 5. Net.Send 改造\n\n```csharp\n// 改造前\npublic static byte[]? Send(string ip, int port, IAsdu asdu)\n{\n    using IExchange exchange = CreateExchange(ip, port);  // 每次新建\n    FrameCodec.SendFrame(exchange, asdu.GetContent());\n    return FrameCodec.ReceiveFrame(exchange);\n}\n\n// 改造后\nprivate static ConnectionPool? _pool;\n\npublic static byte[]? Send(string ip, int port, IAsdu asdu)\n{\n    _pool ??= new ConnectionPool(CreateExchange!);\n    using ExchangeLease lease = _pool.UseClient(ip, port);  // 池化\n    if (lease == null) return null;\n    FrameCodec.SendFrame(lease.Exchange, asdu.GetContent());\n    return FrameCodec.ReceiveFrame(lease.Exchange);\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 6. 对照 RemoteOps\n\n| NetLab | RemoteOps | 说明 |\n|--------|----------|------|\n| `ExchangeLease` | `Extend<IExchange>` | `Helper/Extend.cs` |\n| `PoolBucket` | （无独立类，内联在 Net.cs） | 教学拆出来，RemoteOps 是内联 List |\n| `ConnectionPool` | `Net.cs:115` ConcurrentDictionary | RemoteOps 没有单独池类，全在 Net 静态字段 |\n| `UseClient` | `Net.UseClient` | 逻辑几乎一致 |\n| `Net.Send` | `Net.InternalSend` | 教学版无协商帧（RemoteOps 有） |\n\n---\n\n## 7. 动手练习\n\n### 练习 1：验证池复用\n\n```csharp\n// RunPooledTest() 已经写好\n// 10 次 Net.Send → 只会创建 1~2 个 TCP 连接\ndotnet run --project Client\n```\n\n用 `netstat -an | findstr 9000` 观察实际 TCP 连接数。\n\n### 练习 2：并发压力测试\n\n```csharp\nvar tasks = new List<Task>();\nfor (int i = 0; i < 100; i++)\n{\n    tasks.Add(Task.Run(() =>\n    {\n        Net.Send(\"127.0.0.1\", 9000, new BinaryAsdu(...));\n    }));\n}\nawait Task.WhenAll(tasks);\n// 观察：100 个并发请求，实际只建了几个连接\n```\n\n### 练习 3：模拟连接断开\n\n服务端重启后，客户端池里的旧连接 `IsConnected` 变 false。下一次 `UseClient` 会自动清理并新建。验证这一点。\n\n### 练习 4：改用 Net.Send 替代直接 IExchange\n\n把 `EchoClient.RunTest()` 里的直接 IExchange 方式改为用 `Net.Send` 逐条发送，对比区别。\n\n---\n\n## Phase 3 总结\n\n```\nPhase 2.1: IExchange 接口           → 不再依赖 NetworkStream\nPhase 2.2: 委托注入                 → 全局切换连接方式\nPhase 3:   连接池                   → 连接复用，不每次新建\n```\n\n三个 Phase 共同构成了 RemoteOps `Helper/Net.cs` 的完整教学拆解：\n\n```\nRemoteOps Net.cs:\n  CreateClient 委托  ← Phase 2.2\n  + UseClient 池     ← Phase 3\n  + InternalSend     ← Phase 2.2 + Phase 3 合并\n  + LengthToBytes    ← Phase 1.1（已拆到 FrameCodec）\n```\n",
  "filePath": "D:\\code\\lab\\NetLab\\docs\\tutorials\\05-connection-pool.md"
}
```

| `Client/Net.cs` | 从 EchoClient.cs 拆出独立文件；`Send` 改为 `_pool.UseClient` 池化 |
| `Client/EchoClient.cs` | 删除 Net 类（已迁出）；新增 `RunPooledTest()` 方法 |
| `docs/README.md` | Phase 3 状态更新 |

### 最终结构

```
Client/
├── Program.cs
├── Net.cs                  ← 委托 + 池化 Send
├── ConnectionPool.cs       ← ExchangeLease + PoolBucket + ConnectionPool
├── EchoClient.cs           ← RunTest + RunPooledTest
└── SingleConnectionClient.cs
```

### 三层委托 + 池的关系

```
Net.CreateExchange 委托     →  决定"怎么建"（明文/加密）
ConnectionPool.UseClient    →  决定"什么时候建、什么时候复用"
Net.Send                    →  业务唯一入口（委托 + 池 + 帧协议）
```

你的笔记可以跑 `RunPooledTest()` 验证池效果：

```powershell
# 改 Program.cs 为：
using NetLab.Client;
new EchoClient("127.0.0.1", 9000).RunPooledTest();

# 另一窗口

```

## Assistant (Plan · DeepSeek V4 Pro · 13.5s)

_Thinking:_

The user is asking if there's anything else they need to understand about the connection pool. They've grasped the core concept well:
- One IP:port can have a group of connections
- UseClient acquires/scans for reusable connections
- Also cleans up dead connections
- Dispose returns to pool instead of closing

Let me think about what deeper aspects they might benefit from understanding, but also what's genuinely useful vs. over-explaining.

Key deeper points about this connection pool design:

1. **Why reverse traversal?** (they might not have noticed this detail) - because RemoveAt during forward traversal shifts indices.

2. **Why lock the entire bucket instead of using ConcurrentBag?** - the need for scan + conditional remove + conditional create as an atomic operation.

3. **The pool doesn't limit connections** - no max connection count, no timeout for idle connections. RemoteOps doesn't have these either.

4. **No backpressure** - if processing is slow but requests keep coming, the pool creates more connections, which could exhaust server resources.

5. **The negotiation frame issue in RemoteOps** - RemoteOps' UseClient sends an immediate negotiation frame (BinaryASDU(Business.Equip)), which is a known design flaw. NetLab doesn't replicate this.

6. **Connection stickiness** - the pool naturally creates "sticky" connections per ip:port, which works well for the request-response pattern but could be an issue for load-balanced setups.

7. **The pool is per-process, not distributed** - if you have multiple MainServer processes, each has its own pool.

But the user's understanding is already quite deep. I should:
1. Acknowledge their understanding
2. Mention the key subtle points they might have missed
3. Ask if they want to go deeper on any of these, or move to Phase 4

I should keep it concise since the user dislikes unnecessary verbosity.

你的理解完全准确。补充两个可能没注意到的细节：

**1. 反向遍历的原因**

```csharp
for (int i = bucket.Items.Count - 1; i >= 0; i--)
```

如果正向遍历，RemoveAt 删掉一个后后续元素前移，会跳过下一个。反向遍历不受影响。

**2. 池不限制连接数**

当前设计没有上限、没有空闲超时。高并发时会一直新建连接。RemoteOps 生产代码里也没有，是已知设计缺陷——你可能在 Phase 6（对照生产）时注意到这一点。

---

除此之外你掌握的已经够了。继续 Phase 4（多业务分发）还是先把 `RunPooledTest()` 跑一遍验证？

_Thinking:_

The user is making an observation about the naming. In RemoteOps:

- The same name `CreateClient` is used both for the delegate and sometimes confused with the factory method

In my NetLab implementation:
- `Net.CreateExchange` is the static delegate field
- `ConnectionPool` takes a `_factory` parameter (of type `Net.CreateExchangeFunc`)

The user noticed that I renamed it to `_factory` inside ConnectionPool, which is cleaner naming. They're asking about RemoteOps - in RemoteOps, the same variable name `CreateClient` is used as both the delegate field and sometimes passed around ambiguously.

Let me confirm this and discuss the RemoteOps code pattern. The user seems to be in plan mode - they're asking a conceptual question before we proceed to Phase 4.

In RemoteOps `Helper/Net.cs`:
```csharp
public static CreateClientFunc CreateClient = null;  // Line 113
```

And in `UseClient()`:
```csharp
IExchange client = CreateClient(ip, port);  // Line 136
```

The same static field `CreateClient` is used directly - there's no explicit factory parameter passed to a pool class. The pool and factory are all in one static class. No separation of concerns.

In my teaching version:
- `Net.CreateExchange` is the delegate
- `ConnectionPool` receives a `_factory` in its constructor - clearly naming it as what it is: a factory function

This is better for understanding because it makes the dependency explicit. The user noticed this.

Now they're in plan mode. I should confirm their observation and ask if they want to proceed to Phase 4.

观察得很准。对比一下：

```
RemoteOps Net.cs:
  static CreateClientFunc CreateClient = null;   ← 既是字段名，也是"创建客户端"的语义
  IExchange client = CreateClient(ip, port);     ← 同一个名字，调用时承担了 factory 角色
  → 没有单独 pool 类，factory 和 pool 全混在静态字段里

NetLab 教学版:
  Net.CreateExchange = (ip, port) => { ... };    ← 委托字段，名如其意
  ConnectionPool(Net.CreateExchangeFunc factory)  ← 构造函数参数名 factory，明确职责
  → 池是独立的类，factory 通过构造函数注入
```

RemoteOps 的问题是：同一个文件、同一个变量同时承担了三层含义（工厂、连接池管理器、帧编码工具），没有命名上区分。教学版拆成 `CreateExchange`（字段）+ `_factory`（池用）+ `FrameCodec`（帧），每个名字只做一件事。

## Assistant (Plan · DeepSeek V4 Pro · 40.1s)

_Thinking:_

The user wants to move into Phase 4 - Multi-business dispatch. Let me plan this carefully.

Phase 4 is about handling multiple business types (Manage, File, Agent) on a single TCP port. The key concepts are:

1. **Negotiate frame**: When a connection is established, the client sends a negotiate frame telling the server "I'm here for business type X"
2. **Business enum**: Manage=1, File=2, Agent=3, etc.
3. **IChannel interface**: Different handlers for different business types
4. **Server template method**: `StartupChannel` pattern that reads negotiate frame → dispatches to correct channel

Let me think about how to structure this for NetLab.

### Current state:
- EchoServer accepts connections and echoes back everything
- EchoClient sends messages and receives echoes
- No concept of different business types

### What Phase 4 should add:

1. **Business enum** in Protocol/ (shared)
   ```csharp
   public enum Business : byte
   {
       Manage = 1,
       File = 2,
       Agent = 3,
       Equip = 4
   }
   ```

2. **IChannel interface** - what a business handler looks like
   ```csharp
   public interface IChannel
   {
       void Run(IExchange exchange);
   }
   ```

3. **Server base class** - generic server that dispatches by Business
   ```csharp
   public class BusinessServer
   {
       private Dictionary<Business, Func<IChannel>> _handlers;
       
       public void RegisterProcess(Business business, Func<IChannel> factory);
       public void Start();
   }
   ```

4. **Negotiate frame** - BinaryAsdu with Business byte as content
   - When connection established, client sends `BinaryAsdu(new byte[] { (byte)Business.Manage })`
   - Server reads it, finds the right IChannel, calls `channel.Run(exchange)`

5. **Channel implementations** (demo):
   - `EchoChannel` - behaves like current EchoServer (for Manage business)
   - `FileChannel` - simple stub (for File business)
   - `AgentChannel` - simple stub (for Agent business)

### Code structure changes:

```
Protocol/
├── ...
├── Business.cs              (NEW - Business enum)
├── IChannel.cs              (NEW - channel interface)
├── BusinessServer.cs        (NEW - generic server base)
├── Channels/                (NEW)
│   ├── EchoChannel.cs       (Manage business)
│   ├── FileChannel.cs       (File business)
│   └── AgentChannel.cs      (Agent business)

Server/
├── EchoServer.cs            (replaced by BusinessServer + EchoChannel)
├── ...
```

Actually, wait. Let me think about this more carefully. The Server project currently has EchoServer. I should change it to use the new BusinessServer pattern.

### Key design decisions:

1. **Negotiate frame**: Should be a simple BinaryAsdu with the Business byte. This is exactly what RemoteOps does - the first frame on a new connection is a negotiate frame.

2. **Connection flow**:
   ```
   Client connects
   → Client sends negotiate: BinaryAsdu([0x01])  // Business.Manage
   → Server StartupChannel:
       1. ReceiveFrame → get negotiate bytes
       2. bytes[0] → Business.Manage
       3. Find handler for Business.Manage → new EchoChannel()
       4. channel.ResponseNegotiate(exchange) → send back confirmation
       5. channel.Run(exchange) → main loop
   ```

3. **Where to put things**:
   - `Business` enum and `IChannel` → `Protocol/` (shared)
   - `BusinessServer` → `Protocol/` (shared, or could be in Server/)
   - Channel implementations → `Protocol/Channels/` (shared)
   
   Actually, BusinessServer is server-specific logic. But since it's generic and reusable, Protocol/ makes sense as a shared library.

4. **What about Client side?**
   - Client needs to send negotiate frame after connection
   - Then proceed with normal business messages
   - Could add a `Net.Connect(ip, port, business)` method that creates connection + negotiates

### Revised structure:

```
Protocol/
├── Business.cs
├── IChannel.cs
├── BusinessServer.cs        (generic server that dispatches by Business)
└── Channels/
    ├── EchoChannel.cs       (echo business)

    └── AgentChannel.cs      (stub)

├── EchoServer.cs            (deprecated? or kept as simple version)

Client/
├── EchoClient.cs            (updated to send negotiate frame)
├── Net.cs                   (add Connect method?)
└── ...
```

- `docs/tutorials/06-business-dispatch.md` - single document covering the whole thing

### Simplified approach:

Since this is a learning project, let me keep it practical:

1. **Business enum** - simple byte enum
2. **IChannel** - `ResponseNegotiate(IExchange)` + `Run(IExchange)` 
3. **BusinessServer** - listener + dispatch
4. **Three channel stubs** - EchoChannel (echo), FileChannel (prints "file channel"), AgentChannel (prints "agent channel")
5. **Client update** - send negotiate frame before business messages

Let me think about the specific code design more carefully.

For BusinessServer, the key flow:
```csharp
public class BusinessServer
{
    private readonly Dictionary<Business, Func<IChannel>> _factories = new();
    private readonly int _port;
    
    public void RegisterProcess(Business business, Func<IChannel> factory)
    {
        _factories[business] = factory;
    }
    
    public void Start() { ... }
    
    private void StartupChannel(IExchange exchange)
    {
        // 1. Receive negotiate frame
        byte[]? negotiateBytes = FrameCodec.ReceiveFrame(exchange);
        if (negotiateBytes == null || negotiateBytes.Length == 0) return;
        Business business = (Business)negotiateBytes[0];
        
        // 2. Find handler
        if (!_factories.TryGetValue(business, out var factory)) return;
        IChannel channel = factory();
        
        // 3. Response negotiate
        channel.ResponseNegotiate(exchange, negotiateBytes);
        
        // 4. Run channel
        channel.Run(exchange);
    }
}
```

For IChannel:
```csharp
public interface IChannel
{
    bool ResponseNegotiate(IExchange exchange, byte[] negotiateData);
    void Run(IExchange exchange);
}
```

For EchoChannel (Manage business):
```csharp
public class EchoChannel : IChannel
{
    public bool ResponseNegotiate(IExchange exchange, byte[] negotiateData)
    {
        // Send back confirmation
        FrameCodec.SendFrame(exchange, new byte[] { 0x01 });
        return true;
    }
    
    public void Run(IExchange exchange)
    {
        while (true)
        {
            byte[]? payload = FrameCodec.ReceiveFrame(exchange);
            if (payload == null) break;
            
            // Echo back
            FrameCodec.SendFrame(exchange, payload);
        }
    }
}
```

For Client, Net.Send needs to send negotiate frame first:
```csharp
// Option: Add negotiate to Net.Send
// Or: Have a separate Connect that returns IExchange after negotiation

// I think cleaner: Net.Send should handle negotiation internally
// But that changes semantics... 

// Better: Add Net.Connect that does the negotiation
public static IExchange? Connect(string ip, int port, Business business)
{
    IExchange exchange = CreateExchange(ip, port);
    
    // Send negotiate
    FrameCodec.SendFrame(exchange, new byte[] { (byte)business });
    
    // Wait for response
    byte[]? response = FrameCodec.ReceiveFrame(exchange);
    if (response == null) { exchange.Dispose(); return null; }
    
    return exchange;
}
```

Then EchoClient uses `Net.Connect` to get a negotiated connection.

Let me also think about the document flow. The key insight to convey:

1. **Problem**: One port needs to serve Manage, File, Agent simultaneously
2. **Problem**: A single `while(true) { ReceiveFrame; echo; }` can only handle one business
3. **Solution**: First frame = negotiate (which business?), then dispatch to right handler
4. **Why not separate ports?** Too many ports to manage, firewall rules, etc.
5. **Dispatch mechanism**: Business enum → factory dictionary → IChannel
6. **Exercise**: Add a 4th business type (Monitor)

I think this is a solid plan. Let me present it.

Actually, I should also think about whether to keep the old EchoServer or replace it. The old EchoServer is still there as `Server/EchoServer.cs`. I could either:
a) Keep it and add BusinessServer separately (Program.cs can run either)
b) Replace it entirely

I think (a) is better - keep the simple echo for comparison.

Let me present the plan.

## Phase 4 计划 — 多业务分发

### 问题

当前 `EchoServer` 一条连接只做一件事——echo。但 RemoteOps 里 `ChannelServer` 的 9101 端口同时处理三种业务：

```
同一个端口 9101
  ├── Manage 请求 → ChannelManageProcess（通道状态查询）
  ├── File   请求 → EquipFileProcess（文件下发）
  └── Agent  请求 → EquipBaseAgentProcess（代理隧道）
```

怎么让服务端知道"这个连接是来干嘛的"？

---

### 方案：协商帧 + 业务枚举 + Channel 分发

**第一步 — 发协商帧**

连接建立后，客户端第一帧就是协商帧（`BinaryAsdu([0x01])`），告诉服务端"我是 Manage 业务"。

**第二步 — 分发到对应的 Channel**

```
服务端 Accept
  → ReceiveFrame → 读到 [0x01]
  → [0x01] = Business.Manage
  → 从注册表找 Business.Manage → new EchoChannel()
  → ResponseNegotiate() 回确认
  → channel.Run(exchange) 主循环
```

**第三步 — 不同 Channel 不同行为**

| Business | Channel | 行为 |
|----------|---------|------|
| Manage=1 | EchoChannel | 回显（当前 echo 逻辑） |
| File=2 | FileChannel | 打印 "收到文件请求" |
| Agent=3 | AgentChannel | 打印 "收到代理请求" |

---

### 新增结构

```
Protocol/
├── Business.cs              ← Business 枚举 (byte)
├── IChannel.cs              ← ResponseNegotiate + Run
├── BusinessServer.cs        ← 服务端基类：监听 + 分发
└── Channels/
    ├── EchoChannel.cs       ← Manage 业务（echo）
    ├── FileChannel.cs       ← File 业务（桩）
    └── AgentChannel.cs      ← Agent 业务（桩）

Client/
├── Net.cs                   ← 加 Net.Connect(ip, port, business) 协商连接
├── EchoClient.cs            ← 演示三种业务分别 Connect
```

### `Net.Connect` — 带协商的连接

```csharp
// 新建方法：连接 + 协商 + 返回已协商的连接
public static IExchange? Connect(string ip, int port, Business business)
{
    IExchange exchange = CreateExchange(ip, port);
    FrameCodec.SendFrame(exchange, new byte[] { (byte)business });
    byte[]? response = FrameCodec.ReceiveFrame(exchange);
    if (response == null) { exchange.Dispose(); return null; }
    return exchange;
}
```

### `BusinessServer.StartupChannel` — 服务端分发

```csharp
void StartupChannel(IExchange exchange)
{
    byte[]? data = FrameCodec.ReceiveFrame(exchange);  // 协商帧
    Business biz = (Business)data[0];
    IChannel channel = _factories[biz]();               // 查注册表
    channel.ResponseNegotiate(exchange, data);          // 回确认
    channel.Run(exchange);                              // 主循环
}
```

---

| # | 文件 | 动作 |
|---|------|------|
| 1 | `Protocol/Business.cs` | 新建 — 枚举 |
| 2 | `Protocol/IChannel.cs` | 新建 — 接口 |
| 3 | `Protocol/BusinessServer.cs` | 新建 — 分发服务端 |
| 4 | `Protocol/Channels/EchoChannel.cs` | 新建 — Manage |
| 5 | `Protocol/Channels/FileChannel.cs` | 新建 — File（桩） |
| 6 | `Protocol/Channels/AgentChannel.cs` | 新建 — Agent（桩） |
| 7 | `Client/Net.cs` | 改造 — 加 `Connect` |
| 8 | `Client/EchoClient.cs` | 改造 — 演示 Connect + 多业务 |
| 9 | `Server/Program.cs` | 改为 `BusinessServer` 注册三种 Channel |
| 10 | `docs/tutorials/06-business-dispatch.md` | 新建 |
| 11 | `docs/README.md` | 更新 |

|--------|----------|------|
| `Business` | `Business` | `Protocol/State.cs` |
| `IChannel` | `IChannel` | `Exchange/IChannel.cs` |
| `BusinessServer` | `Server` (abstract) | `Exchange/Server.cs` |
| `EchoChannel` | `EquipManagerProcess` / `ChannelManageProcess` | 各种 Process |

11 项，核心就是一个概念：**第一帧说身份，后续帧做业务**。可以切执行模式了。

---

## User

总体可执行，但有 **3 个关键修正点**，不然 Phase 4 容易讲歪。

## 1. “一条 TCP 连接上同时跑三种业务”这句话要改

更准确是：

```text
同一个监听端口可以接收三种业务连接；
每条 TCP 连接通过第一帧协商，确定自己属于哪一种业务。
```

不是：

```text
一条 TCP 连接上同时跑 Manage / File / Agent
```

除非你要做 **多路复用 multiplexing**，也就是同一条连接里每帧都带业务类型。
但你现在设计的是：

```text
连接建立
  ↓
第一帧：我是 Manage / File / Agent
  ↓
后续整条连接都交给对应 Channel 处理
```

所以这叫 **连接级业务分发**，不是 **帧级多业务复用**。

---

## 2. `Net.Connect` 不应该直接绕过连接池，至少要说明

你写的是：

```csharp
IExchange exchange = CreateExchange(ip, port);
```

如果 Phase 3 已经有连接池，那这里有两种路线：

### 路线 A：Phase 4 先绕过连接池

可以，但文档要明确：

```text
本阶段为了讲清“业务协商 + Channel 分发”，Net.Connect 暂时直接创建连接，不走连接池。
连接池和业务协商的整合放到下一步。
```

### 路线 B：直接接入连接池

那 `Connect` 应该不是直接 `CreateExchange`，而是从池里拿连接。

但这里会有一个麻烦：**池里的连接是否已经协商过业务？**

如果连接池复用连接，就不能随便拿一个旧连接重新发协商帧。
因为旧连接可能已经属于 `Manage`，不能下一次又拿来当 `File`。

所以 Phase 4 教学建议先用 **路线 A**，避免把“连接池复用”和“业务绑定连接”混在一起。

---

## 3. 协商响应要定义清楚

现在写的是：

```csharp
channel.ResponseNegotiate(exchange, data);
```

但没定义它回什么。

建议统一规定：

```text
协商成功：返回 [0x00]
未知业务：返回 [0xFF] 后关闭连接
```

或者：

```text
协商成功：返回原 business byte
协商失败：返回空 / 关闭
```

教学版推荐简单点：

```csharp
public void ResponseNegotiate(IExchange exchange)
{
    FrameCodec.SendFrame(exchange, new byte[] { 0x00 });
}
```

客户端 `Net.Connect` 里检查：

```csharp
if (response == null || response.Length == 0 || response[0] != 0x00)
{
    exchange.Dispose();
    return null;
}
```

---

## 建议后的 Phase 4 定位

这阶段只讲一个核心概念：

```text
同一个端口接收连接；
第一帧说明业务身份；
服务端根据业务类型把连接交给不同 Channel。
```

推荐标题也可以改成：

```text
Phase 4 — 业务协商与 Channel 分发
```

比“多业务分发”更准确。

## 判断

计划可以执行，但先改这三点：

```text
1. 改成“同端口多业务连接”，不要说“一条连接同时跑三种业务”
2. Net.Connect 暂时绕过连接池，并在文档里说明原因
3. 协商成功/失败响应格式固定下来
``` Net.Connect 不应该直接绕过连接池 这块你应该看下原来的代码中究竟是啥样的，究竟是一个端口处理一个业务还是 每次都断开的还是 有其他的处理方式。、
